<h1 class="header">Quotes</h1>
</div>
<div class="header" id="quotes_content">

<div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0397292"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">holds up jar of dirt</span>]
Oi! Fishface! Lose something? Eh? Scungilli! </p><p>
[<span class="fine">falls down stairs, holds up jar again</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
Got it! Come to negotiate, eh? Have you, you slimy git? Look what I got. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">sing-song</span>]
I got a jar of dirt, I got a jar of dirt, and guess what's inside it! </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0397275"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
Land is where you are safe, Jack Sparrow, and so you will carry land with you. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
Dirt. This is a jar of dirt. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
Yes. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
...Is the jar of dirt going to help? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
If you don't want it, give it back. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">greedily</span>]
No! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
Then it helps. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0397277"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0001745/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">'Bootstrap' Bill Turner</span></a>:
Wondering how it's played? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
I understand. It's a game of deception. But your bet includes all the dice, not just your own. What are they wagering? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001745/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">'Bootstrap' Bill Turner</span></a>:
Oh, the only thing we have. Years of service. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
So any crew member can be challenged? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001745/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">'Bootstrap' Bill Turner</span></a>:
Aye. Anyone. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
I challenge Davy Jones. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0631490/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Davy Jones</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">Davy Jones is stepping down the stairs and as he does, barnacles and mussels hanging on the steps retract</span>]
I accept, mate </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0397422"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">while the Pearl's crew and Will are in the bone cages on the cannibal's island</span>]
The Pelagostos made Jack their chief. But he only stays chief so long as he *acts* like a chief </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
So, Jack had no choice. He's as captive as the rest of us. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
Worse, it turns out. See, the Pelagostos believe Jack is a god in human form, and they intend of doing him the honor of releasing him from his fleshy prison. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">Cotton takes Gibbs fingers and bites them to show a point</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
Aaah! They will roast him and eat him. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
Where's the rest of the crew? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">ominously</span>]
These cages we're in... were not built until *after* we got here. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0397296"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
The Pearl's gone, along with its captain. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
And already the world seems a little less bright. He fooled us all, right to the end. But I guess that honest streak finally won out. To Jack Sparrow. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0188871/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ragetti</span></a>:
Never another like Captain Jack. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0034305/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Pintel</span></a>:
He was a gentleman of fortune, he was. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0461136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Elizabeth Swann</span></a>:
He was a good man. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
If there was anything could be done to bring him back... </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
Would you do it? What would any of you do? Would you sail to the ends of the earth and back to fetch back witty Jack, and him precious Pearl? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>,Â <a href="/name/nm0188871/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ragetti</span></a>,Â <a href="/name/nm0034305/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Pintel</span></a>:
Aye! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0461136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Elizabeth Swann</span></a>:
Yes. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
All right. But if you will brave the weird and haunted shores at world's end, then you will need a captain who knows those waters. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001691/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Barbossa</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">enters</span>]
So tell me, what's become of my ship? </p></div>

I took the liberty of filling in my name. </p><p>

[<span class="fine">shakes his head</span>]
Better. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">tosses a bag onto Beckett's desk</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0202603/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Norrington</span></a>:
The heart of Davey Jones. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0397305"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">Jack's hat is tossed overboard by the monkey while the Black Pearl is fleeing the Kraken</span>]
Jack's hat! </p><p>
[<span class="fine">the crew gathers at the rail</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
Clear about! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
No, no! Leave it! </p><p>
[<span class="fine">the whole crew stares at him incredulously</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
Run! </p><p>
[<span class="fine">he runs away</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">he looks at the crew</span>]
Back to yer stations, the lot o' ye! </p><p>
[<span class="fine">he finds Jack hiding underneath the stairs</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
Jack? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
Shhh. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
For the love of Mother and Child, Jack, what's coming after us? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">short pause</span>]
Nothing. </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
Mr. Gibbs. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
Captain. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
We have a need to travel upriver. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
By "need," do you mean a trifling need? Fleeting? As in, say, a passing fancy? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
No, a resolute and unyielding need. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0397331"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0202603/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Norrington</span></a>:
Do excuse me while I kill the man who ruined my life. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
Be my guest. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
Let us examine that claim for a moment, former Commodore, shall we? Who was it that, at the very moment you had a notorious pirate safely behind bars, saw fit to free said pirate and take your dearly beloved all to hisself, eh? So whose fault is it *really* that you've ended up a rum-pot deckhand what takes orders from pirates? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0202603/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Norrington</span></a>:
ENOUGH! </p><p>
[<span class="fine">Jack somersaults off roof, Norrington turns to Will</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0202603/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Norrington</span></a>:
Unfortunately Mr. Turner, he's right! </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0034305/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Pintel</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">watching Norrington, Will and Jack fight whilst Elizabeth is screaming and throwing rocks</span>]
How'd this go all screwy? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0188871/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ragetti</span></a>:
Well, each wants the chest for hisself, don't 'e? Mr. Norrington, I think, is trying to regain a bit of honor. Old Jack's looking to trade it, save his own skin. And Turner there, I think 'e's trying to settle some unresolved business twixt him and his twice-cursed pirate father. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0034305/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Pintel</span></a>:
Sad. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0397404"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0001745/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">'Bootstrap' Bill Turner</span></a>:
It was always in my blood to die at sea, but it was not a fate I ever wanted for you. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
It was not a fate you had to choose for yourself, either. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001745/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">'Bootstrap' Bill Turner</span></a>:
I could say I did what I had to when I left you to go pirating, but it would taste a lie to say it wasn't what I wanted. You owe me nothing. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
They'll know you helped me. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001745/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">'Bootstrap' Bill Turner</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">laughs cynically</span>]
What more can they do to me? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
This is a promise. I'll find a way to sever Jones' hold on you, and not rest until my blade pierces his heat. I will not abandon you. I promise. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0397412"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0390903/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Lord Cutler Beckett</span></a>:
The East India Trading Company has need of your services. We wish for you to act as our agent in a business transaction with our mutual friend Captain Sparrow. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
More acquaintance than friend. How do you know him? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0390903/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Lord Cutler Beckett</span></a>:
We've had dealings in the past. And we've each left out mark on each other. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
What mark did he leave on you? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0390903/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Lord Cutler Beckett</span></a>:
By your efforts, Jack Sparrow was set free. I would like you to go to him and recover a certain property in his position. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
Recover? At the point of a sword? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0390903/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Lord Cutler Beckett</span></a>:
Bargain! You will offer what amounts to a full pardon. Jack will be free. A privateer in the employ of England. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
Somehow I doubt Jack will consider employment the same as being free. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0390903/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Lord Cutler Beckett</span></a>:
Freedom! Jack Sparrow is a dying breed. The world is shrinking. The blank edges of the map filled in. Jack must find his place in the new world or perish. </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">pulls out sword and threatens Will</span>]
Can't let you do that, William. 'Cause if Jones is dead, who's to call his terrible beastie off the hunt, eh? Now, if you please. The key. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">Pulls his sword on Jack</span>]
I keep the promises I make, Jack. I intend to free my father. I hope you're here to see it. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0202603/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Norrington</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">Norrington draws his sword, points it at Will</span>]
I can't let you do that, either. So sorry. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">to Norrington</span>]
I knew you'd warm up to me eventually. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0202603/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Norrington</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">Norrington points his sword at Jack</span>]
Lord Beckett desires the contents of that chest. I deliver it, I get my life back. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
Ah. The dark side of ambition. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0202603/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Norrington</span></a>:
Oh, I prefer to see it as the promise of redemption. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0397280"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
It's funny what a man will do to forestall his final judgment. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001745/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">'Bootstrap' Bill Turner</span></a>:
You made a deal with him too, Jack. He raised the Pearl from the depths for you. Thirteen years you've been her captain. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
Technically... </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001745/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">'Bootstrap' Bill Turner</span></a>:
You won't be able to talk yourself out of this. The terms that apply to me apply to you as well. One soul, bound to crew a hundred years upon his ship. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
Yes, but the Flying Dutchmen already has a captain, so there's really... </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001745/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">'Bootstrap' Bill Turner</span></a>:
Then it's the locker for you! Jones' terrible leviathan will find you, and drag the Pearl back to the depths and you along with it. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
Any idea when Jones might release said terrible beastie? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001745/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">'Bootstrap' Bill Turner</span></a>:
I've already told you, Jack. Your time is up. He comes now. </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0001745/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">'Bootstrap' Bill Turner</span></a>:

<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
I've sworn no oath. </p><p>

[<span class="fine">grasps Will's shoulders</span>]
Then you must get away. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0397344"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
You know of Davy Jones? A man of the sea, a great sailor. Until he run afoul of that which vexes all men. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
What vexes all men? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
What indeed. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
The sea? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0034305/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Pintel</span></a>:
Sums? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0188871/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ragetti</span></a>:
The dichotomy of good and evil? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
A woman. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
A woman. He fell in love. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
No, no, I heard it was the sea he fell in love with. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">annoyed</span>]
Same story, different versions. And all are true. See, it was a woman as changing and harsh and untamable as the sea. Him never stopped loving her. But the pain it caused was to much to live with, but not enough to cause him to die. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0089217/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Will Turner</span></a>:
What exactly did he put into the chest? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
Him heart. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0188871/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ragetti</span></a>:
Literally or figuratively? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0034305/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Pintel</span></a>:
He couldn't literally put his heart in a chest. Could he? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0365140/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Tia Dalma</span></a>:
It was not worth feeling what small, fleeting joy life brings. </p></div>

<a href="/name/nm0000596/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Governor Weatherby Swann</span></a>:

<a href="/name/nm0461136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Elizabeth Swann</span></a>:
A fair trial ends in a hanging. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000596/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Governor Weatherby Swann</span></a>:
Then there is nothing left for you here. </p></div>

[<span class="fine">first lines</span>]
</p><p>

<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
I'll watch yer back. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:

Mind the boat. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0135440/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Cotton's Parrot</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">to Cotton</span>]
Mind the boat. </p><p>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
Gentlemen... what do keys do? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm1258483/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Leech</span></a>:
Keys unlock... things? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
And whatever this key unlocks, inside there's something valuable. So we're setting out to find whatever this key unlocks! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
No. If we don't have the key, we can't open whatever it is we don't have that it unlocks. So what purpose would be served in finding whatever need be unlocked, which we don't have, without first having found the key what unlocks it? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0573618/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Gibbs</span></a>:
So we're going after this key! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000136/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack Sparrow</span></a>:
You're not making any sense at all. </p></div>
